country_event = { #Startup Event
	id = the_command.0
	title = the_command.0.t
	desc = the_command.0.d
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = R62
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			4311 = {
				set_variable = {
					which = command_jade_mines_tension
					value = 50
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = the_command.1
				days = 300
				random = 100
			}
			R63 = { set_country_flag = command_slave_state_flag }
			R64 = { set_country_flag = command_slave_state_flag }
			R65 = { set_country_flag = command_slave_state_flag }
			R66 = { set_country_flag = command_slave_state_flag }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.0.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		add_army_professionalism = 0.2
		
		custom_tooltip = command_mechanics_hint_tt
		# set_country_flag = command_laws_of_ninun_unlocked_flag
	}
}

province_event = { # Orcish slaves in $Provincename$
	id = the_command.2
	title = the_command.2.t
	desc = the_command.2.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		owned_by = R62
		owner = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = the_abolish_slavery_act } }
		has_orcish_minority_trigger = no
		has_orcish_majority_trigger = no
		NOT = {
			has_terrain = cavern
			has_terrain = dwarven_road
			has_terrain = dwarven_hold
			has_terrain = dwarven_hold_surface
			has_terrain = city_terrain
			trade_goods = cloth
			trade_goods = paper
			trade_goods = glass
			trade_goods = chinaware
			trade_goods = slaves
			trade_goods = silk
			trade_goods = dyes
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			OR = {
				trade_goods = tea
				trade_goods = cotton
				trade_goods = spices
				trade_goods = tropical_wood
				trade_goods = tobacco
				trade_goods = sugar
				trade_goods = coffee
				trade_goods = iron
				trade_goods = copper
				trade_goods = gold
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			culture_group = hobgoblin
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			OR = {
				trade_goods = grain
				trade_goods = livestock
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			unrest = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			unrest = 10
		}
	}
	is_mtth_scaled_to_size = 1

	option = { # 
		name = the_command.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		add_permanent_province_modifier = {
			name = orcish_slave_boom
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_orcish_minority_size_effect = yes
		owner = { small_decrease_of_orcish_tolerance_effect = yes }
	}
}

country_event = { # The rule of [ROOT.Monarch.GetName]
	id = the_command.3
	title = the_command.3.t
	desc = the_command.3.desc
	picture = SEJM_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_reform = hobgoblin_stratocracy_reform
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_wolf_command_special_commissions }
				set_country_flag = revoke_wolf_command_special_commissions
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_boar_command_special_commissions }
				set_country_flag = revoke_boar_command_special_commissions
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_lion_command_special_commissions }
				set_country_flag = revoke_lion_command_special_commissions
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_special_commissions }
				set_country_flag = revoke_dragon_command_special_commissions
			}

				limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_special_commissions }
				set_country_flag = revoke_elephant_command_special_commissions

			if = {
				limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_special_commissions }
				set_country_flag = revoke_tiger_command_special_commissions
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # The time of the Wolf has come
		name = the_command.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { dynasty = "Boarborn" }
				NOT = { has_faction = hob_boar_command }
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { dynasty = "Lionborn" }
				NOT = { has_faction = hob_lion_command }
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { dynasty = "Dragonborn" }
				NOT = { has_faction = hob_dragon_command }
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { dynasty = "Elephantborn" }
				NOT = { has_faction = hob_elephant_command }
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { dynasty = "Tigerborn" }
				NOT = { has_faction = hob_tiger_command }
			}
			has_faction = hob_wolf_command
		}

### Magic events

country_event = { #End the Temple's Curse
	id = the_command.4
	title = the_command.4.t
	desc = the_command.4.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = R62
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { OR = { has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex } NOT = { has_province_flag = temple_being_plundered } is_city = yes is_core = ROOT }
				setup_temple_restoration_speed = yes
				save_event_target_as = temple_to_restore
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.4.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		custom_tooltip = command_the_temples_curse_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_temple_complex = yes }
				add_ogre_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
		}
		event_target:temple_to_restore = { begin_temple_restoration = yes }
	}
}

### Jade Mines events

country_event = { #Goblin Infighting
	id = the_command.10
	title = the_command.10.t
	desc = the_command.10.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture
	goto = rebel_target

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = R62
		NOT = { has_country_flag = command_jade_rivalry_ended }
		4311 = {
			check_variable = {
				which = command_jade_mines_tension
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			4311 = {
				check_variable = {
					which = command_jade_mines_tension
					value = 30
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			4311 = {
				check_variable = {
					which = command_jade_mines_tension
					value = 40
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			4311 = {
				check_variable = {
					which = command_jade_mines_tension
					value = 50
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { region = jade_mines_region }
				save_event_target_as = rebel_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.10.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		event_target:rebel_target = {
			spawn_dwarovar_goblin_rebels = { size = 1 }
		}
		
		# 4311 = {
			# change_variable = {
				# which = command_jade_mines_tension
				# value = 1
			# }
		# }
	}
}

### Moving Camp Events

province_event = { #Migration to $PROVINCE$
	id = the_command.20
	title = the_command.20.t
	desc = the_command.20.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
		region = shamakhad_region
		owned_by = R62
		R62 = {
			has_country_flag = command_moving_camp_started_flag
			any_owned_province = {
				region = jade_mines_region
				has_any_hobgoblin_pop_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			province_id = 4635
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			province_id = 4635
			NOT = { culture = lion_command }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				area = khasardul_area
				area = pharata_area
				area = nadida_area
			}
		}
	}
	is_mtth_scaled_to_size = 1

	option = {
		name = the_command.20.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		
		owner = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					region = jade_mines_region
					OR = {
						has_hobgoblin_majority_trigger = yes
						has_hobgoblin_minority_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = { has_hobgoblin_minority_trigger = yes }
					remove_hobgoblin_minority_size_effect = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							NOT = { development = 5 }
							AND = { province_id = 4313 NOT = { development = 17 } } #Vurdriz-Andriz
							AND = { province_id = 4311 NOT = { development = 24 } } #Gronstunad
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { development = 4 }
						random_list = {
							1 = { trigger = { base_tax = 2 } add_base_tax = -1 }
							1 = { trigger = { base_production = 2 } add_base_production = -1 }
							1 = { trigger = { base_manpower = 2 } add_base_manpower = -1 }
						}
					}
					change_culture = undergrowth_goblin
				}
				else = {
					random_list = {
						1 = { trigger = { base_tax = 2 } add_base_tax = -1 }
						1 = { trigger = { base_production = 2 } add_base_production = -1 }
						1 = { trigger = { base_manpower = 2 } add_base_manpower = -1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		ROOT = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_large_hobgoblin_minority_trigger = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { owner = { num_of_owned_provinces_with = { value = 4 culture = lion_command region = shamakhad_region } } }
					random_list = {
						3 = { add_base_tax = 1 }
						3 = { add_base_production = 1 }
						4 = { add_base_manpower = 1 }
					}
				}
				else = {
					random_list = {
						3 =  {
							random_list = {
								3 = { add_base_tax = 1 }
								3 = { add_base_production = 1 }
								4 = { add_base_manpower = 1 }
							}
						}
						1 = {
							change_culture = lion_command
							change_religion = godlost
							hidden_effect = { on_province_culture_converted_estate_privilges_effect = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_hobgoblin_majority_trigger = yes }
				random_list = {
					3 = { add_base_tax = 1 }
					3 = { add_base_production = 1 }
					4 = { add_base_manpower = 1 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_hobgoblin_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #The Laws of Ninun
	id = the_command.34
	title = the_command.34.t
	desc = the_command.34.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		owned_by = R62
		OR = {
			AND = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = command_laws_of_ninun_unlocked_flag
					ai = yes
				}
				any_neighbor_province = {
					OR = {
						culture_group = hobgoblin
						culture_group = wuhyun
					}
				}
			}
			has_state_edict = laws_of_ninun_edict
		}
		OR = {
			culture_is_human = yes
			culture_is_half_orcish = yes
			culture_is_orcish = yes
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { culture_group = wuhyun }
			NOT = { religion = godlost }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 18
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			culture_group = wuhyun
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			religion = godlost
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 25
			owner = { ai = yes }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.34.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		trigger = { NOT = { culture_group = wuhyun } }
		
		if = {
			limit = { continent = asia }
			export_to_variable = {
				which = original_wuhyun_culture
				value = culture
				who = ROOT
			}
		} # for sunrise empire to convert wuhyun back

		random_list = {
			1 = {
				trigger = { NOT = { has_orcish_majority_trigger = yes } }
				if = {
					limit = { superregion = rahen_superregion }
					change_culture = kusonin
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { 
						OR = {
							superregion = yanshen_superregion
							superregion = north_haless_superregion
						}
					}
					change_culture = ikaniwagain
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { superregion = south_haless_superregion }
					change_culture = kintonan
				}
				else = {
					change_culture = rinonokegyun
				}
			}
			2 = {
				trigger = {
					owner = { has_country_flag = R62_honourable_half_orcs_flag }
					OR = {
						has_orcish_majority_trigger = yes
						has_any_half_orcish_pop_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				change_culture = wuhyun_half_orc
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { on_province_culture_converted_estate_privilges_effect = yes }
	}
	option = {
		name = the_command.34.b
		trigger = { NOT = { religion = godlost } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}

		if = {
			limit = { continent = asia }
			export_to_variable = {
				which = original_wuhyun_religion
				value = religion
				who = ROOT
			}
		} # for sunrise empire to convert wuhyun back

		change_religion = godlost
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					area_for_scope_province = {
						type = all
						OR = {
							AND = {
								religion = godlost
								culture_group = wuhyun
							}
							AND = {
								culture_is_human = no
								OR = {
									AND = {
										owner = { has_country_flag = R62_honourable_half_orcs_flag }
										culture_is_half_orcish = no
										culture_is_orcish = no
									}
									NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = R62_honourable_half_orcs_flag } }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				province_event = {
					id = the_command.55
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Obedience or Consensus
	id = the_command.43
	title = the_command.43.t
	desc = the_command.43.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = the_command.43.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		add_government_reform = command_obedience
	}
	option = {
		name = the_command.43.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		add_government_reform = command_consensus
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_wolf_command_war_room_rights } }
				remove_faction = hob_wolf_command
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_boar_command_war_room_rights } }
				remove_faction = hob_boar_command
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_lion_command_war_room_rights } }
				remove_faction = hob_lion_command
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_war_room_rights }
				add_faction = hob_dragon_command
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_war_room_rights }
				add_faction = hob_elephant_command
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_war_room_rights }
				add_faction = hob_tiger_command
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Tughayasa Petition
	id = the_command.44
	title = the_command.44.t
	desc = the_command.44.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = command_tughayasa_petition_open_flag
	}
	
	option = { #The War Room is full enough
		name = the_command.44.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					has_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_war_room_rights
					has_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_war_room_rights
					has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_war_room_rights
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_war_room_rights
						has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_war_room_rights
					}
					AND = {
						has_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_war_room_rights
						has_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_war_room_rights
					}
					AND = {
						has_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_war_room_rights
						has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_war_room_rights
					}
				}
			}
			add_absolutism = 5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_war_room_rights
					has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_war_room_rights
					has_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_war_room_rights
				}
			}
			add_absolutism = 10
		}
		else = {
			add_absolutism = 15
		}
		
		clr_country_flag = command_tughayasa_petition_open_flag
	}
	option = { #That concludes our meeting
		name = the_command.44.e
		trigger = {
			has_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_war_room_rights
			has_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_war_room_rights
			has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_war_room_rights
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		clr_country_flag = command_tughayasa_petition_open_flag
	}
	
	option = { #The Dragon Command earned their place
		name = the_command.44.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		set_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_war_room_rights
	}
	option = { #The Elephant Command earned their place
		name = the_command.44.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		set_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_war_room_rights
	}
	option = { #The Tiger Command earned their place
		name = the_command.44.d
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		set_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_war_room_rights
	}
	
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = command_tughayasa_petition_open_flag }
			country_event = { id = the_command.4400 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Fate of the Oracle
	id = the_command.46
	title = the_command.46.t
	desc = the_command.46.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Kill the oracle
		name = the_command.46.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		add_legitimacy_or_monarch_power = { VAL = 30 }
		
		# add_country_modifier = {
			# name = command_killed_the_oracle_command
			# duration = -1
		# }
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_known_country = {
					has_reform = raja_reform
				}
			}
			random_known_country = {
				limit = { has_reform = raja_reform }
				add_stability = -1
				add_aggressive_expansion = { who = ROOT value = 25 apply_calc = no }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = command_killed_the_oracle_raja
					duration = 5475
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = command_fate_of_the_oracle_kill_tt
		tooltip = {
			random_known_country = {
				limit = {
					capital_scope = {
						OR = {
							superregion = rahen_superregion
							superregion = yanshen_superregion
							superregion = south_haless_superregion
						}
					}
					NOT = { has_reform = raja_reform }
					NOT = {
						alliance_with = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				add_stability = -1
				add_aggressive_expansion = { who = ROOT value = 25 apply_calc = no }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = command_killed_the_oracle_other
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_known_country = {
				limit = {
					capital_scope = {
						OR = {
							superregion = rahen_superregion
							superregion = yanshen_superregion
							superregion = south_haless_superregion
						}
					}
					NOT = { has_reform = raja_reform }
					NOT = {
						alliance_with = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				add_stability = -1
				add_aggressive_expansion = { who = ROOT value = 25 apply_calc = no }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = command_killed_the_oracle_other
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Chain the oracle
		name = the_command.46.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		add_stability = -1
		add_legitimacy = -20
		custom_tooltip = command_fate_of_the_oracle_enslave_tt
		set_country_flag = command_enslaved_the_oracle_flag
	}
	option = { # leave the oracle free
		name = the_command.46.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		add_stability = -1
		add_legitimacy = -20
		
		custom_tooltip = command_fate_of_the_oracle_kill_tt
		tooltip = {
			random_known_country = {
				limit = {
					capital_scope = {
						OR = {
							superregion = rahen_superregion
							superregion = yanshen_superregion
							superregion = south_haless_superregion
						}
					}
					NOT = { has_reform = raja_reform }
					NOT = {
						alliance_with = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				add_aggressive_expansion = { who = ROOT value = -10 apply_calc = no }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_known_country = {
				limit = {
					capital_scope = {
						OR = {
							superregion = rahen_superregion
							superregion = yanshen_superregion
							superregion = south_haless_superregion
						}
					}
					NOT = { has_reform = raja_reform }
					NOT = {
						alliance_with = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				add_aggressive_expansion = { who = ROOT value = -10 apply_calc = no }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Command demands subjugation from the Oni!
	id = the_command.49
	title = the_command.49.t
	desc = the_command.49.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes

	option = { #accept
		name = the_command.49.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		R62 = {
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = slave_state
				subject = Y01
			}
			command_change_korashi_supply = { increase = yes }
			hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = command_slave_state_flag }
		}
		Y01 = {
			release_all_subjects = yes
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { NOT = { region = demon_hills_region } }
				cede_province = R62
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #refuse, which will give them the azjakuma campaign
		name = the_command.49.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		Y01 = { break_alliance = R62 }
		R62 = { country_event = { id = the_command.50 } }
		add_trust = {
			who = R62
			value = -40
			mutual = yes
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #Wuhyunification of slave-state land
	id = the_command.51
	title = the_command.51.t
	desc = the_command.51.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		owner = { 
			is_subject_of_type_with_overlord = { 
				who = R62
				type = slave_state 
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = R62_slave_state_wuhyunification_flag
		OR = {
			has_human_majority_trigger = yes
			has_half_orcish_majority_trigger = yes
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { culture_group = wuhyun }
			NOT = { religion = godlost }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 60
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			culture_group = wuhyun
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			religion = godlost
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.34.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		trigger = { NOT = { culture_group = wuhyun } }
		
		if = {
			limit = { continent = asia }	
			export_to_variable = {
				which = original_wuhyun_culture
				value = culture
				who = ROOT
			}
		} #for sunrise empire to convert wuhyun back

		random_list = {
			1 = {
				trigger = { NOT = { has_orcish_majority_trigger = yes } }
				if = {
					limit = { superregion = rahen_superregion }
					change_culture = kusonin
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { 
						OR = {
							superregion = yanshen_superregion
							superregion = north_haless_superregion
						}
					}
					change_culture = ikaniwagain
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { superregion = south_haless_superregion }
					change_culture = kintonan
				}
				else = {
					change_culture = rinonokegyun
				}
			}
			2 = {
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						has_orcish_majority_trigger = yes
						has_any_half_orcish_pop_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				change_culture = wuhyun_half_orc
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { on_province_culture_converted_estate_privilges_effect = yes }
	}
	option = {
		name = the_command.34.b
		trigger = { NOT = { religion = godlost } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}

		if = {
			limit = { continent = asia }
			export_to_variable = {
				which = original_wuhyun_religion
				value = religion
				who = ROOT
			}
		} # for sunrise empire to convert wuhyun back

		change_religion = godlost
	}
}

country_event = { #Reform 1
	id = the_command.60
	title = the_command.60.t
	desc = the_command.60.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = the_command.60.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		
		add_country_modifier = { name = command_reform_a duration = -1 }
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = command_reform_a_passed
					has_country_flag = command_reform_b_passed
					has_country_flag = command_reform_c_passed
					has_country_flag = command_reform_d_passed
					has_country_flag = command_reform_e_passed
					
					has_country_flag = command_reform_f_passed
					has_country_flag = command_reform_g_passed
					has_country_flag = command_reform_h_passed
					has_country_flag = command_reform_i_passed
					has_country_flag = command_reform_j_passed
				}
				clr_country_flag = command_reform_a_passed
				clr_country_flag = command_reform_b_passed
				clr_country_flag = command_reform_c_passed
				clr_country_flag = command_reform_d_passed
				clr_country_flag = command_reform_e_passed
				
				clr_country_flag = command_reform_f_passed
				clr_country_flag = command_reform_g_passed
				clr_country_flag = command_reform_h_passed
				clr_country_flag = command_reform_i_passed
				clr_country_flag = command_reform_j_passed
				
				clr_country_flag = command_the_ten_reforms_flag
				clr_country_flag = command_the_ten_reforms_menu_open_flag
				set_country_flag = command_the_ten_reforms_completed_flag
				
				remove_country_modifier = command_reform_a
				remove_country_modifier = command_reform_b
				remove_country_modifier = command_reform_c
				remove_country_modifier = command_reform_d
				# remove_country_modifier = command_reform_e
				remove_country_modifier = command_reform_f
				# remove_country_modifier = command_reform_g
				remove_country_modifier = command_reform_h
				remove_country_modifier = command_reform_i
				# remove_country_modifier = command_reform_j
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = command_the_ten_reforms
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

			}
		}

		}

country_event = { #Chandra of the Many Hands comes out in the open
	id = the_command.84
	title = the_command.84.t
	desc = the_command.84.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = { R09 = { exists = no } 4467 = { owned_by = ROOT } }
					
					4467 = {
						add_core = R09
						every_neighbor_province = {
							limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
							add_core = R09
						}
						area = {
							limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
							add_core = R09
						}
					}
					release_with_religion_and_culture = { tag = R09 religion = high_philosophy culture = rajnadhid }
					R09 = { save_event_target_as = mage_rebel_nation }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { R12 = { exists = no } 4509 = { owned_by = ROOT } }
					
					4509 = {
						add_core = R12
						every_neighbor_province = {
							limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
							add_core = R12
						}
						area = {
							limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
							add_core = R12
						}
					}
					release_with_religion_and_culture = { tag = R12 religion = high_philosophy culture = rajnadhid }
					R12 = { save_event_target_as = mage_rebel_nation }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = {
						OR = { 
							R09 = { exists = yes }
							NOT = { 4467 = { owned_by = ROOT } }
						}
						OR = { 
							R12 = { exists = yes }
							NOT = { 4509 = { owned_by = ROOT } }
						}
					}
					
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								culture = shandibad
								culture = rajnadhid
								culture = sobhagand
								culture = muthadhaya
							}
						}
						add_core = R73
						every_neighbor_province = {
							limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
							add_core = R73
						}
						area = {
							limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
							add_core = R73
						}
					}
					release_with_religion_and_culture = { tag = R73 religion = high_philosophy culture = shandibad }
					R73 = { save_event_target_as = mage_rebel_nation }
				}
			}
			
			event_target:mage_rebel_nation = {
				override_country_name = THE_MANY_HANDS_REBELLION
				change_government = theocracy
				add_government_reform = magocracy_reform
				change_religion = high_philosophy
				
				capital_scope = {
					spawn_units_for = {
						amount = 22
						type = infantry
						who = event_target:mage_rebel_nation
					}
					spawn_units_for = {
						amount = 4
						type = cavalry
						who = event_target:mage_rebel_nation
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { mil_tech = 13 } }
						spawn_units_for = {
							amount = 10
							type = artillery
							who = event_target:mage_rebel_nation
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { total_development = 1600 } }
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = { NOT = { infantry_in_province = event_target:mage_rebel_nation } }
						spawn_units_for = {
							amount = 18
							type = infantry
							who = event_target:mage_rebel_nation
						}
						spawn_units_for = {
							amount = 4
							type = cavalry
							who = event_target:mage_rebel_nation
						}
						if = {
							limit = { ROOT = { mil_tech = 13 } }
							spawn_units_for = {
								amount = 8
								type = artillery

							}
						}
					}
				}

country_event = { #Hidden annexation event, needs no loc
	id = the_command.90
	title = the_command.90.t
	desc = the_command.90.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		any_known_country = {
			has_country_flag = mage_rebel_nation
			capital_scope = {
				controlled_by = ROOT
				has_siege = no
			}
			NOT = {
				war_score_against = {
					who = ROOT
					value = -50
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_known_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = mage_rebel_nation
				capital_scope = {
					controlled_by = ROOT
					has_siege = no
				}
				NOT = {
					war_score_against = {
						who = ROOT
						value = -50
					}
				}
			}
			restore_country_name = yes
			clr_country_flag = mage_rebel_nation
			ROOT = { inherit = PREV }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.90.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		
	}
}

country_event = { # Thunderfist Movement Menu
	id = the_command.100
	title = the_command.100.t
	desc = the_command.100.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = command_move_menu_open_flag
		
			command_generate_move_target_canditates = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # Choose first
		name = the_command.100.a
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_flag = command_move_target_candidate_1
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		goto = command_move_target_candidate_1
		
		command_move_orc_slave_state = {
			tag = R63
			target = command_move_target_candidate_1
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = command_move_menu_open_flag
		}
	}

	option = { # Choose second
		name = the_command.100.b
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_flag = command_move_target_candidate_2
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		goto = command_move_target_candidate_2
		
		command_move_orc_slave_state = {
			tag = R63
			target = command_move_target_candidate_2
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = command_move_menu_open_flag
		}
	}

	option = { # Choose third
		name = the_command.100.c
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_flag = command_move_target_candidate_3
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		goto = command_move_target_candidate_3
		
		command_move_orc_slave_state = {
			tag = R63
			target = command_move_target_candidate_3
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = command_move_menu_open_flag
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = the_command.100.dd
		highlight = yes
		
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = command_move_menu_open_flag
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				clr_province_flag = command_move_target_candidate_1
				clr_province_flag = command_move_target_candidate_2
				clr_province_flag = command_move_target_candidate_3
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

		name = the_command.201.a
		ai_chance = {

		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = ronin_executed
			4941 = {
				remove_province_modifier = hobgoblin_minority_oppressed_small
				remove_province_modifier = hobgoblin_minority_oppressed_large
				remove_province_modifier = hobgoblin_minority_coexisting_small
				remove_province_modifier = hobgoblin_minority_coexisting_large
				remove_province_modifier = hobgoblin_minority_integrated_small
				remove_province_modifier = hobgoblin_minority_integrated_large
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = executing_ronin_tooltip
		4941 = {
			add_devastation = 35
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = the_command.301
	title = the_command.301.t
	desc = the_command.301.desc
	picture = COUNTRY_COLLAPSE_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Domestic Teachings
		name = the_command.301.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_personal_deity = domestic_teachings
				has_personal_deity = domestic_teachings_improved
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				faction_in_power = hob_lion_command
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = command_new_schools_of_thought_flag }
			change_personal_deity = domestic_teachings_improved
		}
		else = {
			change_personal_deity = domestic_teachings
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Strict Teachings

	id = the_command.312
	title = the_command.312.t
	desc = the_command.312.desc
	picture = COUNTRY_COLLAPSE_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = command_armies_menu_2_open
		hidden_effect = {
			1 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Nevermind
		name = flavor_castanor_go_back
		highlight = yes
		clr_country_flag = command_armies_menu_2_open
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = the_command.310 } }
	}
	option = { #Restock army manpower
		name = the_command.312.a
		
		command_army_resupply = { command = wolf }
	}
	option = { #Settle down troops
		name = the_command.312.b
		
		command_army_settle_down = { command = wolf }
	}
	option = { #Special Ability
		name = the_command.312.c
		
		command_army_special_ability_wolf = yes
	}
	
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = command_armies_menu_2_open }
			country_event = { id = the_command.313 }
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = the_command.350
	title = the_command.350.t
	desc = the_command.350.d
	picture = COUNTRY_COLLAPSE_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { 
		name = the_command.350.a
		
		clr_country_flag = command_founding_new_command_flag
		command_new_command_effect = yes
		change_estate_land_share = {
			estate = estate_dragon_command
			share = 12
		}
		set_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_land_rights
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_wolf_command_act_of_division
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_lion_command_act_of_division
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_boar_command_act_of_division
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_act_of_division
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_act_of_division
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_act_of_division
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = the_command.1000
	title = the_command.1000.t
	desc = the_command.1000.desc
	picture = NOBLE_ESTATE_DEMANDS_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_reform = hobgoblin_stratocracy_reform
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					kanzad_area = { type = all is_city = yes }
					dwarovrod_51_53_area = { type = all is_city = yes }
					grozumdihr_area = { type = all is_city = yes }
					ovdal_az_an_area = { type = all is_city = yes }
					dwarovrod_57_59_area = { type = all is_city = yes }
					hul_az_krakazol_area = { type = all is_city = yes }
					dwarovrod_63_65_area = { type = all is_city = yes }
				}
				set_country_flag = command_tree_of_stone_campaign_unlocked_flag
			}
			
			
			pick_random_estate_if_present = { flag = present_agenda estate_action = generate_estate_agenda }
			pick_random_estate_if_present = { flag = present_agenda estate_action = generate_estate_agenda }
			pick_random_estate_if_present = { flag = present_agenda estate_action = generate_estate_agenda }
		}
	}

	after = {
		clr_country_flag = estate_wolf_command_present_agenda
		clr_country_flag = estate_boar_command_present_agenda
		clr_country_flag = estate_lion_command_present_agenda
		clr_country_flag = estate_dragon_command_present_agenda
		clr_country_flag = estate_elephant_command_present_agenda
		clr_country_flag = estate_tiger_command_present_agenda
		clr_country_flag = estate_gerunanin_present_agenda
		clear_estate_agenda_cache = ROOT
		
		clr_country_flag = disable_first_lion_command_agenda_flag
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.1000.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = estate_wolf_command_present_agenda
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					command_has_potential_campaign = yes
					command_has_available_wolf_campaign = no
				}
			}
		}
		start_estate_agenda = estate_wolf_command
		goto = estate_wolf_command
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						loyalty = 30
						estate = estate_wolf_command
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						loyalty = 20
						estate = estate_wolf_command
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				estate_influence = {
					influence = 70
					estate = estate_wolf_command
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_absolutism_active = yes
				num_of_estate_privileges = {
					estate = estate_wolf_command
					value = 1
				}
				estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_wolf_command
					higher_than_influence = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = the_command.1000.b

	}

		hidden_effect = {

				}
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_wolf_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 1 } } }
					1 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {

	}
	
	immediate = {

				}

				}

				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_dragon_command }
					4 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_tiger_command }

				}
				1 = {

			}

				faction = hob_wolf_command
				influence = 10
			}
			add_estate_influence_modifier = {
				estate = estate_wolf_command
				desc = EST_VAL_COMMAND_WAR_ROOM_SUPPORT
				influence = 10
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 2 } }
			#effects for estate_boar_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_boar_command
				loyalty = 15
			}
			add_faction_influence = {
				faction = hob_boar_command
				influence = 10
			}
			add_estate_influence_modifier = {
				estate = estate_boar_command
				desc = EST_VAL_COMMAND_WAR_ROOM_SUPPORT
				influence = 10
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 3 } }
			#effects for estate_lion_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_lion_command
				loyalty = 15
			}
			add_faction_influence = {
				faction = hob_lion_command
				influence = 10
			}
			add_estate_influence_modifier = {
				estate = estate_lion_command
				desc = EST_VAL_COMMAND_WAR_ROOM_SUPPORT
				influence = 10
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 4 } }
			#effects for estate_dragon_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_dragon_command
				loyalty = 15
			}
			add_faction_influence = {
				faction = hob_dragon_command
				influence = 10
			}
			add_estate_influence_modifier = {
				estate = estate_dragon_command
				desc = EST_VAL_COMMAND_WAR_ROOM_SUPPORT
				influence = 10
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 5 } }

country_event = { #Mediate in marriage negotiations
	id = the_command.1004
	title = the_command.1004.t 
	desc = the_command.1004.desc 
	picture = NOBLE_ESTATE_DEMANDS_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_reform = hobgoblin_stratocracy_reform
		has_country_flag = command_war_room
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_wolf_command }
					1 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_boar_command }
					2 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_lion_command }
					3 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_dragon_command }
					4 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_tiger_command }
					5 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_elephant_command }
					6 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_wolf_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 1 } } }
					1 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_boar_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 2 } } }
					2 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_lion_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 3 } } }
					3 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_dragon_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 4 } } }
					4 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_tiger_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 5 } } }
					5 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_elephant_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 6 } } }
					6 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = the_command.1004.a
		
		if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 1 } }
			#effects for estate_wolf_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_wolf_command
				loyalty = 10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 2 } }
			#effects for estate_boar_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_boar_command
				loyalty = 10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 3 } }
			#effects for estate_lion_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_lion_command
				loyalty = 10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 4 } }
			#effects for estate_dragon_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_dragon_command
				loyalty = 10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 5 } }
			#effects for estate_tiger_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_tiger_command
				loyalty = 10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 6 } }
			#effects for estate_elephant_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_elephant_command
				loyalty = 10
			}
		}

				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_elephant_command }
					6 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_wolf_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 1 } } }
					1 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_boar_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 2 } } }
					2 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_lion_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 3 } } }
					3 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_dragon_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 4 } } }
					4 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_tiger_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 5 } } }
					5 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_faction = hob_elephant_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 6 } } }
					6 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = the_command.1007.a
		
		if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 1 } }
			#effects for estate_wolf_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_wolf_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 2 } }
			#effects for estate_boar_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_boar_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 3 } }
			#effects for estate_lion_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_lion_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 4 } }
			#effects for estate_dragon_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_dragon_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 5 } }
			#effects for estate_tiger_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_tiger_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 6 } }
			#effects for estate_elephant_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_elephant_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		
		kill_leader = { type = general }
		add_army_tradition = -5
		add_legitimacy = 5
	}
	option = { 
		name = the_command.1007.b
		
		if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_2 = { province_id = 1 } }
			#effects for estate_wolf_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_wolf_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_2 = { province_id = 2 } }
			#effects for estate_boar_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_boar_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_2 = { province_id = 3 } }
			#effects for estate_lion_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_lion_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_2 = { province_id = 4 } }
			#effects for estate_dragon_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_dragon_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_2 = { province_id = 5 } }
			#effects for estate_tiger_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_tiger_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_2 = { province_id = 6 } }
			#effects for estate_elephant_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_elephant_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		
		add_legitimacy = -5
	}
}

#starts the tickup
country_event = {
	id = the_command.1984
	title = the_command.1984.t
	desc = the_command.1984.d
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {	
		mission_completed = R62_the_tiger_command
		mission_completed = R62_the_dragon_command
		mission_completed = R62_the_elephant_command
		mission_completed = R62_the_jade_march
		has_estate = estate_tiger_command
		has_estate = estate_dragon_command
		has_estate = estate_elephant_command
		# Requires each subcontinent to have 400 dev owned + over 2k dev outside of Shamakhad.
		OR = {
			development_in_provinces = {
				value = 400
				superregion = yanshen_superregion
			}
			AND = {
				development_in_provinces = {
					value = 200
					superregion = yanshen_superregion
				}
				development_in_provinces = { value = 2000 NOT = { region = shamakhad_region } }
			}
			ai = yes
		}
		development_in_provinces = {
			value = 400
			superregion = south_haless_superregion
		}
		development_in_provinces = {
			value = 400
			superregion = rahen_superregion
			NOT = { region = shamakhad_region }
		}
		development_in_provinces = { value = 1600 NOT = { region = shamakhad_region } }
		any_owned_province = {
			superregion = rahen_superregion
			NOT = { region = shamakhad_region }
			has_terrain = city_terrain
		}
		any_owned_province = {
			superregion = yanshen_superregion
			has_terrain = city_terrain
		}
		any_owned_province = {
			superregion = south_haless_superregion
			OR = {
				has_terrain = city_terrain
				province_id = 4559
				province_id = 4565
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = insubordination_start_flag  set_country_flag = insubordination_be_nice } }
	
	option = {
		name = the_command.1984.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_tooltip = command_1984_tt
		add_stability = -1
		add_legitimacy = -10
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = command_estate_pain
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}

	picture = GENERALS_DISCUSSING_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		had_country_flag = {
			flag = insubordination_start_flag
			days = 750
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = insubordination_complete
			has_country_flag = insubordination_active_flag
			exists = R67
		}
	}

	option = {		# favor lion
		name = the_command.1987.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = command_lions_favored
			duration = 1825
		}
		add_estate_loyalty = {
		    estate = estate_tiger_command
		    loyalty = -10
		}
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_tiger_command
			desc = EST_VAL_LION_COMMAND_FAVORED
			influence = -10
    		duration = 1825
		}
	}
	option = {		# favor tiger
		name = the_command.1987.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = command_tigers_favored
			duration = 1825
		}
		add_estate_loyalty = {
		    estate = estate_lion_command
		    loyalty = -10
		}
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_lion_command
			desc = EST_VAL_TIGER_COMMAND_FAVORED
			influence = -10
    		duration = 1825
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # spawning the tiger command
	id = the_command.1991
	title = the_command.1991.t
	desc = the_command.1991.d
	picture = NUSANTARA_THRONE_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 2
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			has_disaster_progress = {
				disaster = command_insubordination
				value = 80
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = insubordination_start_flag
		OR = {
			NOT = { estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_tiger_command loyalty = 30 } }
			has_disaster_progress = {
				disaster = command_insubordination
				value = 80
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = insubordination_complete }
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = { # Tiger Command breaks free
				limit = {
					superregion = rahen_superregion
					NOT = { region = shamakhad_region }
				}
				add_core = R67
				set_local_autonomy = 0
			}
			release_with_religion_and_culture = { tag = R67 religion = godlost culture = tiger_command } # release the tiger!
			create_subject = { subject_type = subsidiary_command  subject = R67 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_hired_mercenary_company = {
						template = merc_command_tiger_army
					}
				}
				random_hired_mercenary_company = {
					limit = {
						template = merc_command_tiger_army
					}
					disband_mercenary_company = THIS
				}
			}
			R67 = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = command_tiger_buff
					duration = -1
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { development_of_overlord_fraction = 0.25 } R62 = { ai = no } }
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = command_fl_max
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { development_of_overlord_fraction = 0.50 } R62 = { ai = no } }
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = command_fl_mid
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { development_of_overlord_fraction = 0.75 } R62 = { ai = no } }
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = command_fl_min
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				define_general = {
					shock = 4
					fire = 5
					manuever = 6
					siege = 4
					female = yes
					name = "Mishya Tigerborn"
				}
				define_general = {
					shock = 7
					fire = 2
					manuever = 6
					siege = 2
					name = "Kabkuri 'of the Raj' Tigerborn"
				}
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Zurshin"
					dynasty = "Tigerborn"
					adm = 6
					dip = 4
					mil = 3
					female = no
					culture = tiger_command
					religion = godlost
					age = 45
				}
				add_ruler_personality = tactical_genius_personality
				add_ruler_personality = martial_educator_personality
				add_ruler_personality = inspiring_leader_personality
				define_ruler_to_general = {
				    fire = 3
				    shock = 5
				    manuever = 6
				    siege = 2
				}

				set_government_rank = 2
				add_government_reform = hobgoblin_stratocracy_reform
				add_army_professionalism = 1
				add_army_tradition = 50
				add_legitimacy = 100
				add_manpower = 200
				add_treasury = 2000
				add_yearly_manpower = 5
				add_years_of_income = 5
				add_adm_power = 400
				add_dip_power = 400
				add_mil_power = 400
				
				remove_faction = hob_wolf_command
				remove_faction = hob_boar_command
				remove_faction = hob_lion_command

				create_alliance = R68
				create_alliance = R69
				add_historical_friend = R68
				add_historical_friend = R69
			}
			if = {
				limit = { R67 = { is_core = 4411 } }
				R67 = { set_capital = 4411 capital_scope = { save_global_event_target_as = tiger_command_capital } }
				4426 = { save_global_event_target_as = tiger_command_upstream }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { R67 = { is_core = 4435 } }
				R67 = { set_capital = 4435 capital_scope = { save_global_event_target_as = tiger_command_capital } }
				4373 = { save_global_event_target_as = tiger_command_upstream }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { R67 = { is_core = 4409 } }
				R67 = { set_capital = 4409 capital_scope = { save_global_event_target_as = tiger_command_capital } }
				4491 = { save_global_event_target_as = tiger_command_upstream }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { R67 = { is_core = 4420 } }
				R67 = { set_capital = 4420 capital_scope = { save_global_event_target_as = tiger_command_capital } }
				4409 = { save_global_event_target_as = tiger_command_upstream }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { R67 = { is_core = 4391 } }
				R67 = { set_capital = 4391 capital_scope = { save_global_event_target_as = tiger_command_capital } }
				4381 = { save_global_event_target_as = tiger_command_upstream }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { R67 = { is_core = 4485 } }
				R67 = { set_capital = 4485 capital_scope = { save_global_event_target_as = tiger_command_capital } }
				4487 = { save_global_event_target_as = tiger_command_upstream }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { R67 = { is_core = 4380 } }
				R67 = { set_capital = 4380 capital_scope = { save_global_event_target_as = tiger_command_capital } }
				4382 = { save_global_event_target_as = tiger_command_upstream }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { R67 = { is_core = 4367 } }
				R67 = { set_capital = 4367 capital_scope = { save_global_event_target_as = tiger_command_capital } }
				4378 = { save_global_event_target_as = tiger_command_upstream }
			}
			every_subject_country = {	# Transferring Raheni subjects to Tiger Command
				limit = { capital_scope = { superregion = rahen_superregion NOT = { region = shamakhad_region } } }
				if = {
					limit = { is_subject_of_type = autonomous_vassal }
					R67 = { create_subject = { subject = PREV subject_type = autonomous_vassal } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { is_subject_of_type = march }
					R67 = { create_march = PREV }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { is_subject_of_type = client_vassal }
					R67 = { create_subject = { subject = PREV subject_type = client_vassal } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { is_subject_of_type = client_march }
					R67 = { create_subject = { subject = PREV subject_type = client_march } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { is_subject_of_type = slave_state NOT = { primary_culture = wuhyun_half_orc } }
					R67 = { create_subject = { subject = PREV subject_type = slave_state } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { primary_culture = wuhyun_half_orc }
					add_prestige = 10
				}
				else = {
					R67 = { vassalize = PREV }
				}
			}
			R67 = {
				country_event = {
					id = the_command.2002
					days = 31
				}
				every_owned_province = { # delete the forts
					limit = { fort_level = 2 }
					remove_building = fort_15th
					remove_building = fort_16th
					remove_building = fort_17th
					remove_building = fort_18th
				}
				every_owned_province = { # add back the forts
					limit = {
						OR = {
							province_id = 4469
							province_id = 4508
							province_id = 4504
							province_id = 4450
							province_id = 4446
							province_id = 4444
							province_id = 4438
							province_id = 4435
							province_id = 4411
							province_id = 4362
							province_id = 4499
							province_id = 4493
							province_id = 4492
							province_id = 4485
							province_id = 4425
							province_id = 4420
							province_id = 4419
							province_id = 4404
							province_id = 4380
							province_id = 4367
							province_id = 4414
						}
						NOT = { fort_level = 1 }
					}
					add_latest_building = { builder = R67 fort = yes }
				}
				capital_scope = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = command_capital_stronghold_t1
						duration = -1
					}
					set_province_flag = command_tiger_capital_flag
					random_neighbor_province = {
						limit = {
							has_terrain = farmlands
							owned_by = R67
						}
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = command_tiger_warcamp
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = the_command.1991.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}
}

					siege = 1
					female = yes
					name = "Ibawasu Dragonborn"
				}

				    female = yes
				}

				add_government_reform = hobgoblin_stratocracy_reform

				add_legitimacy = 100
				add_manpower = 200
				add_treasury = 2000
				add_yearly_manpower = 5
				add_years_of_income = 5
				add_adm_power = 400
				add_dip_power = 400
				add_mil_power = 400

				remove_faction = hob_boar_command
				remove_faction = hob_lion_command

				create_alliance = R67
				create_alliance = R68
				add_historical_friend = R67
				add_historical_friend = R68

			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = shuvuush_support_command_flag }
				R69 = {
					add_adm_power = 400
					add_dip_power = 400
					add_mil_power = 400
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = command_shuvuush_support
						duration = 1825
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { R69 = { is_core = 4859 } }
				R69 = { set_capital = 4859 capital_scope = { save_global_event_target_as = dragon_command_capital } }
				4853 = { save_global_event_target_as = dragon_command_upstream }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { R69 = { is_core = 4868 } }
				R69 = { set_capital = 4868 capital_scope = { save_global_event_target_as = dragon_command_capital } }
				4873 = { save_global_event_target_as = dragon_command_upstream }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { R69 = { is_core = 4871 } }
				R69 = { set_capital = 4871 capital_scope = { save_global_event_target_as = dragon_command_capital } }
				4869 = { save_global_event_target_as = dragon_command_upstream }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { R69 = { is_core = 4846 } }
				R69 = { set_capital = 4846 capital_scope = { save_global_event_target_as = dragon_command_capital } }
				4845 = { save_global_event_target_as = dragon_command_upstream }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { R69 = { is_core = 4842 } }
				R69 = { set_capital = 4842 capital_scope = { save_global_event_target_as = dragon_command_capital } }
				4826 = { save_global_event_target_as = dragon_command_upstream }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { R69 = { is_core = 4826 } }
				R69 = { set_capital = 4826 capital_scope = { save_global_event_target_as = dragon_command_capital } }
				4818 = { save_global_event_target_as = dragon_command_upstream }
			}
			every_subject_country = {	# Transferring Yansheni subjects to Dragon Command
				limit = { 
					capital_scope = { superregion = yanshen_superregion } 
					NOT = { tag = Y01 }	# Azjakuma is special
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_subject_of_type = autonomous_vassal }
					R69 = { create_subject = { subject = PREV subject_type = autonomous_vassal } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { is_subject_of_type = march }
					R69 = { create_march = PREV }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { is_subject_of_type = client_vassal }
					R69 = { create_subject = { subject = PREV subject_type = client_vassal } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { is_subject_of_type = client_march }
					R69 = { create_subject = { subject = PREV subject_type = client_march } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { is_subject_of_type = slave_state NOT = { primary_culture = wuhyun_half_orc } }
					R69 = { create_subject = { subject = PREV subject_type = slave_state } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { primary_culture = wuhyun_half_orc }
					add_prestige = 10
				}
				else = {
					R69 = { vassalize = PREV }
				}
			}
			R69 = {
				country_event = {
					id = the_command.2002
					days = 31
				}
				every_owned_province = { # delete the forts
					limit = { fort_level = 2 }
					remove_building = fort_15th
					remove_building = fort_16th
					remove_building = fort_17th
					remove_building = fort_18th
				}
				every_owned_province = { # add back the forts
					limit = {
						OR = {
							province_id = 4901
							province_id = 4826
							province_id = 4842
							province_id = 4846
							province_id = 4976
							province_id = 4859
							province_id = 4855
							province_id = 4824
							province_id = 4951
							province_id = 4838
							province_id = 4868
							province_id = 4871
							province_id = 4930
							province_id = 4923
							province_id = 4925
							province_id = 4889
							province_id = 4879
							province_id = 4931
							province_id = 5420
							province_id = 4979
							province_id = 4977
						}
						NOT = { fort_level = 1 }
					}
					add_latest_building = { builder = R69 fort = yes }
				}
				capital_scope = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = command_capital_stronghold_t1
						duration = -1
					}
					set_province_flag = command_dragon_capital_flag
					random_neighbor_province = {
						limit = {
							has_terrain = farmlands
							owned_by = R69
						}
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = command_dragon_warcamp
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = the_command.1993.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}
}

country_event = { # disaster ends
	id = the_command.2010
	title = the_command.2010.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = insubordination_bad } }
		desc = the_command.2010.d
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = insubordination_bad }
		desc = the_command.2010.d.2
	}
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = insubordination_complete
			clr_country_flag = insubordination_active_flag
			clr_country_flag = gobbos_will_remember_this_flag
			remove_country_modifier = command_estate_pain
			remove_country_modifier = command_oni_infiltrators
			event_target:dragon_command_capital = {
				remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t1
				remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t2
				remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t3
				remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t4
				clr_province_flag = command_destroyed_logistics_flag
				clr_province_flag = command_encircled_flag
			}
			event_target:elephant_command_capital = {
				remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t1
				remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t2
				remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t3
				remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t4
				clr_province_flag = command_destroyed_logistics_flag
				clr_province_flag = command_encircled_flag
			}
			event_target:tiger_command_capital = {
				remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t1
				remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t2
				remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t3
				remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t4
				clr_province_flag = command_destroyed_logistics_flag
				clr_province_flag = command_encircled_flag
			}
			R67 = {
				remove_country_modifier = command_tiger_buff
				remove_country_modifier = command_fl_max
				remove_country_modifier = command_fl_mid
				remove_country_modifier = command_fl_min
			}
			R68 = {
				remove_country_modifier = command_elephant_buff
				remove_country_modifier = command_fl_max
				remove_country_modifier = command_fl_mid
				remove_country_modifier = command_fl_min
			}
			R69 = {
				remove_country_modifier = command_dragon_buff
				remove_country_modifier = command_fl_max
				remove_country_modifier = command_fl_mid
				remove_country_modifier = command_fl_min
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns = 4504 }
				4504 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = command_tiger_warcamp
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns = 4613 }
				4613 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = command_elephant_warcamp
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns = 4952 }
				4952 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = command_dragon_warcamp
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # good ending
		name = the_command.2010.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = insubordination_bad } }
		add_legitimacy = 100
		add_army_professionalism = 0.25
		add_war_exhaustion = -10
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = command_jingo_fervor
			duration = 3650
		}
	}
	option = { # bad ending
		name = the_command.2010.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = { has_country_flag = insubordination_bad }
		add_stability = -2
		kill_ruler = yes
		if = {
			limit = { exists = R67 }
			custom_tooltip = command_2010_tt_b
			hidden_effect = {
				west_rajnadhaga_area = {
					limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
					cede_province = R67
					add_core = R67
				}
				tiltaghar_area = {
					limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
					cede_province = R67
					add_core = R67
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			white_peace = R67
			white_peace = R68
			white_peace = R69
			R67 = { grant_independence = yes }
			R68 = { grant_independence = yes }
			R69 = { grant_independence = yes }
		}
	}
}

# Convert new vassals to slave states
# Moved from on_dependency_gained to prevent crashes
country_event = {
	id = the_command.3000
	title = the_command.3000.t
	desc = the_command.3000.d
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
		
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
		
	option = {
		name = the_command.3000.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

		overlord = { create_subject = { subject_type = slave_state subject = ROOT } }
	}
}

# Convert slave states to vassals for non-hobgoblins
# Moved from on_dependency_gained to prevent crashes
country_event = {
        id = the_command.3001
        title = the_command.3001.t
        desc = the_command.3001.d
        picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture

        is_triggered_only = yes
        hidden = yes

        option = {
                name = the_command.3001.a
                ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

                overlord = { create_subject = { subject_type = vassal subject = ROOT } }
        }
}
